At 14:00 on March 19, 2022,

Lane 500 of Xingle Road (except No. 83) has ushered in an official solution.

After nearly 5 days of closed management, it is about to return to the right place. Here, to understand, support and cooperate with the epidemic.

Thank you and your family for the prevention and control work!

We fully understand your desire to let go at this moment, but "unblocking" does not mean "unblocking" or "low wind".

"Risk" does not mean "zero risk". At present, the epidemic prevention and control situation at home and abroad is still severe and complex, and personal protection is still

However, you can't relax. For your health and epidemic prevention and control needs, I would like to give you the following tips:

1, March

From 19 to March 29, please do a good job of self-health monitoring as required.

Report personal temperature and health status to the community twice a day.

2. Please cooperate to complete the nucleic acid testing. The testing time is March 22 and March 29 and will be completed in time.

Report it to the community.

3. Please strengthen personal health protection and develop good hygiene habits such as standardizing the amount of wearing and washing hands frequently. Do it.

Don't pile up, gather, eat together, and cooperate with prevention and control measures such as verification, code scanning and temperature measurement in entering and leaving public places.

4. If the body has abnormal symptoms such as fever, cough-choo-choo and shortness of breath, please wear a slip and go to the nearest medical treatment in time.

The institution went to the fever clinic and informed the medical staff in time that it had carried out sealing and control management.

5. I need to remind you in particular that according to the requirements of epidemic prevention and control in Shanghai, it is necessary not to leave the country.

Why don't you leave Shanghai? According to the Law of the People's Republic of China on the Prevention and Control of Infectious Diseases and the Shanghai Office for the Prevention and Control of Infectious Diseases

The relevant provisions of the Law, if you violate the relevant epidemic prevention requirements, you will be investigated for legal responsibility. This is that you and we do not

I would like to see it.

With everyone's joint efforts, we have shown our determination to work together to overcome difficulties and help each other.

It also makes us deeply understand the difficulty of "restarting". Say "thank you" solemnly to everyone! Thank you for your accumulation.

With great cooperation and selfless dedication, the closed-loop investigation task was successfully completed!

monica albertini  13:44

Dear neighbors,

I sent out the following announcements to the parents of the children I support. I thought you may find it handy for your own children as well!

As we approach this rainy weekend, we continue to be in lockdown and have limited access to activities and resources to support our children. We can spend hours swimming through the internet in search of quality content suitable for our children. We know how busy you are, so we have done a bit of that for you. Below you will find some great, mostly online, and free-of-charge resources for you. They are all interactive, educational, and vital right now as we juggle all the challenges we are facing.


https://www.nasa.gov/stem/forstudents/k-4/index.html

Visitors can download printable storybooks, drive rovers on Mars, learn about astronauts, and navigate a virtual clubhouse fit with puzzles, coloring projects, various spacecraft, and even a calculator that shows your age and weight on other planets and moons. There are also fun STEM projects for elementary school students to complete at home, like making a cloud mobile or learning how to safely land your marshmallow astronaut.

https://www.amnh.org/explore/ology/paleontology#hands-on

Search for fossils, learn to draw a Stegosaurus, play the calls of your favorite prehistoric critters, and so much more. 

https://www.tvokids.com/school-age/our-planet/videos/boredom-buster-nature-craft

It’s a fun way to expose kids to things like magnets, gravity, density, and experiments you can put together at home.

https://icanradio.org/programs/

Tune in for everything from poetry, music, and literature from all over the globe to story time, dance parties, and lullaby hour.


https://icanradio.org/programs/on-demand/the-complete-works-of-winnie-the-pooh/
Complete Winnie the Pooh stories. A delight!


https://kids.nationalgeographic.com

You and the kids may be stuck to your yards or the nearby park, but you can still explore exotic locations via National Geographic. 

https://redyarnproductions.com/videos/

An interactive sing-along variety show that includes puppets, dance parties, and refreshingly woke commentary about our current pandemic situation. 

https://www.pbs.org/parents/activity-finder/ages-all/topics-all/shows-all/types-birthday-party+coloring-and-printable+craft-and-experiment+recipe+games-and-apps

It’s equal parts activities for kids and guidance for parents.


https://www.seussville.com/parents/

Devoted to both parents and educators where you can access things like recipes, crafts, activities, and printable media and arts projects.

monica albertini  07:55

@Jonathan #16 I am very sorry to hear about your daughter’s friend. What a terrifying experience for her and all of those who loved her! Unfortunately, it is a reality for so many. As a counselor that works with children, teens, and their families, I see it every day. The current lockdown measures prioritize certain safety aspects while ignoring others that are central to wellbeing. Humans are mammals. We need contact, connections, purpose, choice, and joy to remain healthy and balanced. A person who cannot meet those needs consistently over extended periods has a marked decrease in their mental health—rates of anxiety and depression soar, much like rates of aggressive behaviors. Social skills weakened. There is significant evidence that cognitive skills decline, especially in older adults. Social connection is protection against many of these conditions and illnesses. Research shows that people with increased rates of anxiety and depression are more prone to physical diseases. With less physical activity, socialization, and time outdoors, circadian rhythms are disrupted and impact sleep. Sleep decline affects immunity. In short, long-term lockdown disrupts all areas of our lives.

尽锐出战，
以快制快，

用最短时间褐制疫情扩散，
上海的封控清零的速度要加快，象浦东这样的一封再封的拖拉局面要改变了，要尽快地把“阳性”清理出来，做到“四应四尽”，即应检尽检，应收尽收，应隔尽隔，应冶尽治，无一遗漏，然后达到小区，街道，区域尽快解封，因此.从今天起，凡工作人员，（包括医护人员，警察，志愿者等凡在门外可走动人员）首先人人做核酸，一人一管，快速检测出结果，而封在家里不外出走动的人员先在家采用测坑原，有疑问的再做核酸，并且是一人一管（不再是20人一管）达到快速出结果，这样就可使封控的时间压缩，快速检出阳性，快速清零，快速解封，而不再是反复检测，封控时间一再拖迤（不会再加7天，加14天的反复封控）
这就是孙春兰所传达出的
“尽锐出战，以快制快，用最短时间褐制疫情扩散”的新精神，

平安是福  21:48

近期小区内各类团购数量激增， 快递、外卖、团购过程中存在感染风险，为有效防止疫情传播，保障小区居民的身体健康和生命安全，现对小区生活物资采购及配送做出如下提示，自发布时起执行:
一、	所有采购物资以满足基本生活条件和确保食品来源可溯、安全卫生为原则，减少不必要的购买。
二、	所有团购必须在组团前向物业中心报备，报备时需明确品种、数量并提供上海市疫情防控生活物资保障企业证明等材料。若有车辆配送需提供车辆通行证，货物送达时配送人员需出示48小时内核酸阴性证明；（目前已成团的接龙请于4月7日17:00前将订购清单提供至管家，未收到订单将不予接收）
三、	组团成功后需在到货前一天将订购明细以Excel格式发送至管家微信，以便提前安排货物配送。若无订购清单，物业管理服务中心将拒绝接收。
四、	所有进入小区物资由工作人员统一消杀后配送。天气逐渐升温，为保证大家收到货物质量，门岗拒绝接受时效较短的物资（如冰淇淋、奶油、鱼虾等易变质食物）。
五、	小区每日需配送外来生活物资数量较多，目前108号楼还需固定值守，物业配送人手有限，因此每日生活物资上午、下午各集中配送一次，生鲜会优先配送，烦请大家耐心等待。
目前小区处于封控状态，对园区采取的管理措施将对广大业主生活带来不便影响，但是为了小区的安全和健康，希望广大业主积极配合物业工作，共同创建安全小区。特殊时期，请各住户共体时艰，共度难关！

平安是福  21:50
